<p>The <b>1996 Men's Olympic Football Tournament</b>, played as part of the <a href="/wiki/1996_Summer_Olympics" title="1996 Summer Olympics">1996 Summer Olympics</a>, was hosted in <a href="/wiki/Birmingham,_Alabama" title="Birmingham, Alabama">Birmingham, Alabama</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C" title="Washington, D.C">Washington, D.C</a>, <a href="/wiki/Orlando,_Florida" title="Orlando, Florida">Orlando, Florida</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Miami,_Florida" title="Miami, Florida">Miami, Florida</a> and <a href="/wiki/Athens,_Georgia" title="Athens, Georgia">Athens, Georgia</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> From <a href="/wiki/1996_Summer_Olympics" title="1996 Summer Olympics">1996</a> onwards, male competitors must be under 23 years old, with three over-23 players allowed per squad. The tournament features 16 men's national teams from the six continental confederations. The 16 teams are drawn into four groups of four and each group plays a <a href="/wiki/Round-robin_tournament" title="Round-robin tournament">round-robin tournament</a>. At the end of the group stage, the top two teams advanced to the knockout stage, beginning with the quarter-finals and culminating with the gold medal match at <a href="/wiki/Sanford_Stadium" title="Sanford Stadium">Sanford Stadium</a> on August 3, 1996.</p>
<p></p>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Quarter-finals">Quarter-finals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Football_at_the_1996_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Quarter-finals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="vevent" style="width: 100%; background-color: transparent; clear:both">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Goalscorers">Goalscorers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Football_at_the_1996_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Goalscorers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>With six goals, Hernán Crespo of Argentina and Bebeto of Brazil are the top scorers in the tournament. In total, 90 goals were scored by 55 different players, with three of them credited as own goals.</p>
<dl>
<dt>6 goals</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina"><img alt="Argentina" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Hern%C3%A1n_Crespo" title="Hernán Crespo">Hernán Crespo</a></li>
